1b1('bum): @#shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa/ bam po nyis
1b2('bum): brgya gyi gsum pa/ / / bcom ldan 'das de ci'i slad du zhe na/ chos kyi dbying
1b3('bum): la ni rnam par rtog pa de dag ma mchis te/ gzugs kyang chos kyi dbyings ma
2a1('bum): lags/ gzugs las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi
2a2('bum): dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs so// tshor ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ tshor ba las
2a3('bum): gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshor
2a4('bum): ba'o/ / 'du shes kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ 'du shes las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis
2b1('bum): te'adu shes nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'du shes so// 'du byed kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags//
2b2('bum): 'du byed las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 'du byed nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'du
2b3('bum): byed do/ / rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rnam par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te//
2b4('bum): rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'o// mig kyang chos kyi dbyings ma
2b5('bum): lags/ mig las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mig nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid
3a1('bum): kyang mig go/ rna ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rna ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rna ba nyid
3a2('bum): kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'o// sna'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sna las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma
3a3('bum): mchis te/ sna nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'o// lce'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lce las gud na'ang
3a4('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lce nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'o// lus kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags//
3a5('bum): lus las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lus nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus so// yid nyid
3a6('bum): kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ yid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ yid nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
3b1('bum): nyid kyang yid do/ / gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ gzugs las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang
3b2('bum): gzugs so/ / sgra'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sgra las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ sgra nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sgra'o// dri'ang chos kyi dbying
3b3('bum): ma lags/ dri las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ dri nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dri'o// ro'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ ro las gud na'ang chos kyi
3b4('bum): dbyings ma mchis te/ ro nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ro'o// reg kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ reg las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ reg nyid kyang
3b5('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang reg go// chos kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ chos las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ chos nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
3b6('bum): dbyings nyid kyang chos so/ / mig gi rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mig gi rnam par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mig gi rnam par shes pa nyid
3b7('bum): kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig gi rnam par shes pa'o// rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rna ba'i rnam par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi
4a1('bum): dbyings ma mchis te/ rna ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'o// sna'i rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi
4a2('bum): dbyings ma lags/ sna'i rnam par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ sna'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'i rnam par
4a3('bum): shes pa'o/ / lce'i rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lce'i rnam par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lce'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
4a4('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'i rnam par shes pa'o// lus kyi rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lus kyi rnam par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/
4a5('bum): lus kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus kyi rnam par shes pa'o// yid kyi rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ yid kyi rnam par
4a6('bum): shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o// mig gi 'dus te reg
4a7('bum): pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig
4b1('bum): gi 'dus te reg pa'o/ / rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos
4b2('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbying ma mchis te
4b3('bum): sna'i 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'i 'dus te reg pa'o// lce'i 'dus te reg pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa
4b4('bum): las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'i 'dus te reg pa'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'ang chos kyi
4b5('bum): dbyings ma lags/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'o//
4b6('bum): yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
4b7('bum): dbyings nyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'o/ / mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings
5a1('bum): ma mchis te/ mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// rna ba'i
5a2('bum): 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor
5a3('bum): bapa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sna'i 'dus te/
5a4('bum): reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'i 'dus te reg
5a5('bum): pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o/ / lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/
5a6('bum): lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'ang
5a7('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
5b1('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor
5b2('bum): pab las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor
5b3('bum): ba'o/ / sa'i khams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sa'i khams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ sa'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang
5b4('bum): sa'i khams so/ / chu'i khams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ chu'i khams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ chu'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid
5b5('bum): kyang chu'i khams so/ / me'i khams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ me'i khams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings pa mchis te/ me'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
5b6('bum): nyid kyang me'i khams so/ / rlung gi khams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rlung gi khams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rlung gi khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
5b7('bum): dbyings nyid kyang rlung gi khams so/ / nam mkha'i khams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ nam mkha'i khams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ nam mkha'i khams nyid kyang
6a1('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang nam mkha'i khams so// rnam par shes pa'i khams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rnam par shes pa'i khams las//
6a2('bum): gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam par shes pa'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'i khams so// ma rig pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma
6a3('bum): lags/ ma rig pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ ma rig pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ma rig pa'o// 'du byed kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags
6a4('bum): 'du byed las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 'du byed nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'du byed do// rnam par shes pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rnam
6a5('bum): par shes pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'o// ming dang gzugs kyang chos kyi dbyings
6a6('bum): ma lags/ ming dang gzugs las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ ming dang gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ming dang gzugs so// skye mched
6a7('bum): drug kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ skye mched drug las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ skye mched drug nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang skye mched drug
6b1('bum): go/ reg pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ reg pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang reg pa'o// tshor ba'ang
6b2('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ tshor ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshor ba'o// sred pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma
6b3('bum): lags/ sred pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ sred pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sred pa'o// len pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ len pa
6b4('bum): las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ len pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang len pa'o// srid pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ srid pa las gud na'ang
6b5('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ srid pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang srid pa'o// skye ba'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ skye ba las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma
6b6('bum): mchis te/ skye ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang skye ba'o// rga shi'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rga shi las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rga shi
6b7('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rga shi'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las gang na'ang chos kyi dbyings
7a1('bum): ma mchis te/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang
7a2('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid
7a3('bum): kyang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ bzod pa'i
7a4('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ brtson 'grus kyi
7a5('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// /
7a6('bum): bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang
7a7('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las gud
7b1('bum): na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// nang stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings
7b2('bum): ma lags/ nang stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ nang stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang nang stong pa nyid do// phyi stong pa nyid kyang chos
7b3('bum): kyi dbyings ma lags/ phyi stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ phyi stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang phyi stong pa nyid do// phyi nang stong pa
7b4('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ phyi nang stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ phyi nang stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang phyi nang stong pa
7b5('bum): nyid do/ / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
7b6('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid do// chen po stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ chen po stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ chen po stong pa
7b7('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang chen po stong pa nyid do// don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ don dam pa stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings
8a1('bum): ma mchis te/ don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang don dam pa stong pa nyid do// 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags
8a2('bum): 'dus byas stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'dus byas stong pa nyid do// 'dus ma byas stong
8a3('bum): pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'dus
8a4('bum): ma byas stong pa nyid do/ / mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mtha' las 'das pa
8a5('bum): stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mtha' las pa stong pa nyid do// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong
8a6('bum): pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do// dor ba med pa stong
8a7('bum): pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ dor ba med pa stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ dor ba med pa med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dor/
8b1('bum): ba med pa stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings
8b2('bum): so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ chos thams cad stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/
8b3('bum): chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang chos thams cad stong pa nyid do// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rang gi mtshan nyid
8b4('bum): stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid do// mi dmigs pa stong pa
8b5('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mi
8b6('bum): dmigs pa stong pa nyid do/ / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyang
8b7('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dngos po med pa stong pa nyid do// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyis las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma
9a1('bum): mchis te/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi
9a2('bum): dbyings ma lags/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
9a3('bum): nyid kyang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do/ / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis
9a4('bum): te/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams so// yang dag par spong ba rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags
9a5('bum): yang dag par spong ba rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ yang dag par spong ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yang dag par spong ba rnams so// rdzu 'phrug
9a6('bum): gyi rkang pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
9a7('bum): dbyings nyid kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams so/ / dbang po rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ dbang po rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ dbang ba rnams kyang chos
9b1('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dbang po rnams so// stobs rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ stobs rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ stobs nyid kyang /
9b2('bum): chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang stobs rnams so// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbying
9b3('bum): ma mchis te/ byang chub kyi yan lag nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams so// lam yang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lam las gud na'ang
9b4('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lam nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lam mo// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ 'phags pa'i bden pa
9b5('bum): rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams so// bsam gtan rnams
9b6('bum): kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ bsam gtan rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ bsam gtan nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang bsam gtan rnams
9b7('bum): so/ / tshad med pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ tshad med pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ tshad med pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
10a1('bum): nyid kyang tshad med pa rnams so/ / gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams las
10a2('bum): gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams so//
10a3('bum): rnam par thar pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rnam par thar pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam par thar pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
10a4('bum): nyid kyang rnam par thar pa rnams so/ / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams las gud na'ang
10a5('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams so// rnam
10a6('bum): par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa
10a7('bum): las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par
10b1('bum): thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'o// mngon par shes pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mngon par shes pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbying/
10b2('bum): ma mchis te/ mngon par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mngon par shes pa rnams so// ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ ting nge 'dzin
10b3('bum): rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ ting nge 'dzin nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ting nge 'dzin rnams so// gzungs kyi sgo rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings
10b4('bum): ma lags/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ gzungs kyi sgo nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzungs kyi sgo rnams so// de bzhin
10b5('bum): gshegs pa'i stobs rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs nyid kyang
10b6('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams so// mi 'jigs pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mi 'jigs pa rnams las gud na'ang chos
10b7('bum): kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mi 'jigs pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mi 'jigs pa rnams so// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags//
11a1('bum): so so yang dag par rig pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ so so yang dag par rig pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang
11a2('bum): so so yang dag par rig pa rnams so/ / byams pa chen po'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ byams pa chen po las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ byams pa chen po nyid kyang chos kyi
11a3('bum): dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang byams pa chen po'o// snying rje chen po'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ snying rje chen po las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ snying rje chen
11a4('bum): po nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang snying rje chen po'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres
11a5('bum): pa rnams las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams
11a6('bum): so/ / rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos
11a7('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'o// lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu las gud
11b1('bum): na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras
11b2('bum): bu'ang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang
11b3('bum): phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o/ / dgra bcom pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ dgra bcom pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ dgra bcom pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
11b4('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dgra bcom pa nyid do// rang byang chub kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rang byang chub las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rang byang chub nyid kyang chos kyi
11b5('bum): dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rang byang chub bo// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma
11b6('bum): mchis te/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid do// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma
11b7('bum): lags/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las gud na'ang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam pa
12a1('bum): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ ji skad du smras pa de bzhin
12a2('bum): no/ / gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs so// tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshor ba'o// 'du shes nyid kyang chos
12a3('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'du shes so// 'du byed nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'du byed do// rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
12a4('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'o// mig nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig go// rna ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'o//
12a5('bum): sna nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'o// lce nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'o// lus nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
12a6('bum): nyid kyang lus so/ / yid nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yid do// gzugs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs so// sgra nyid kyang
12a7('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sgra'o// dri nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dri'o// ro nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ro'o//
12b1('bum): reg nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang reg go// chos nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang chos so// mig gi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
12b2('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig gi rnam par shes pa'o// rna ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'o// sna'i rnam par shes pa
12b3('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'i rnam par shes pa'o// lce'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'i rnam par shes
12b4('bum): pa'o/ / lus kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus kyi rnam par shes pa'o// yid kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
12b5('bum): dbyings nyid kyang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o/ / mig gi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig gi 'dus te reg pa'o// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang
12b6('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'i 'dus te reg pa'o// lce'i
12b7('bum): 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'i 'dus te reg pa'o// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus
13a1('bum): kyi 'dus te reg pa'o/ / yid kyi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen
13a2('bum): gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
13a3('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sna'i 'dus te reg
13a4('bum): ba'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o/ / lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// lus kyi 'dus te
13a5('bum): reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang
13a6('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// sa'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sa'i khams so//
13a7('bum): chu'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang chu'i khams so// me'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang me'i khams so// rlung gi khams
13b1('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rlung gi khams so// nam mkha'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang nam mkha'i khams so// rnam par
13b2('bum): shes pa'i khams nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'i khams so// ma rig pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ma rig pa'o//
13b3('bum): 'du byed nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'du byed do// rnam par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'o// ming dang gzugs
13b4('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ming dang gzugs so// skye mched drug nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang skye mched drug go// reg pa nyid kyang chos
13b5('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang reg pa'o// tshor ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshor ba'o// sred pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid
13b6('bum): kyang sred pa'o/ / len pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang len pa'o// srid pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang srid pa'o// skye ba nyid kyang
13b7('bum): chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang skye ba'o// rga shi nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rga shi'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
14a1('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu
14a2('bum): phyin pa'o/ / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
14a3('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// /
14a4('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// nang stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid
14a5('bum): kyang nang stong pa nyid do/ / phyi stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang phyi stong pa nyid do// phyi nang stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang phyi nang
14a6('bum): stong pa nyid do/ / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid do// chen po stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings
14a7('bum): nyid kyang chen po stong pa nyid do/ / don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang don dam pa stong pa nyid do// 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
14b1('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'dus byas stong pa nyid do// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid do// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa/
14b2('bum): nyid chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang thog ma dang
14b3('bum): tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do/ / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dor ba med pa stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so
14b4('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do/ / chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang chos thams cad stong pa nyid do// rang gi mtshan nyid
14b5('bum): stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid do// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mi dmigs
14b6('bum): pa stong pa nyid do/ / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dngos po med pa stong pa nyid do// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos
14b7('bum): kyi dbyings nyid kyang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do/ / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do// dran pa
15a1('bum): nye bar gzhag pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams so// yang dag par spong ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos
15a2('bum): kyi dbyings nyid kyang yang dag par spong ba rnams so/ / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams so// dbang po nyid kyang chos kyi
15a3('bum): dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dbang po rnams so// stobs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang stobs rnams so// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyang chos kyi
15a4('bum): dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams so// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'phags pa'i lam
15a5('bum): yan lag brgyad pa'o/ / 'phags pa'i bden pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang 'phags pa'i bden// mas so// bsam gtan nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
15a6('bum): dbyings nyid kyang bsam gtan rnams so/ / tshad med pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshad med pa rnams so// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa nyid kyang chos
15a7('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams so// rnam par thar pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par thar pa rnams
15b1('bum): so/ / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams so// rnam par thar pa'i sgo
15b2('bum): stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa
15b3('bum): med pa'o/ / mngon par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mngon par shes pa rnams so// ting nge 'dzin nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang
15b4('bum): ting nge 'dzin rnams so/ / gzungs kyi sgo nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzungs kyi sgo rnams so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so//
15b5('bum): chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams so// mi 'jigs pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mi 'jigs pa rnams so// so so yang dag par
15b6('bum): rig pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang so so yang dag par rig pa rnams so// byams pa chen po nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang byams pa
15b7('bum): chen po'o/ / snying rje chen po nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang snying rje chen po'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid
16a1('bum): kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams so/ / rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'o//
16a2('bum): lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
16a3('bum): dbyings nyid kyang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o/ / dgra bcom pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dgra bcom pa'o// rang byang chub nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi
16a4('bum): dbyings nyid kyang rang byang chub bo/ / lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid do// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang chos
16a5('bum): kyi dbyings so/ / chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do// rab 'byor gal te yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu

16a7('bum): chos kyi dbyings yin pas/ de'i phyir byang chu sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings su shes nas/ chos thams
16b1('bum): cad ming med pa la ming gi brdas chos ston te/ 'di ni gzugs zhes bya'o// 'di ni tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni 'du shes zhes bya'o// 'di ni 'du byed ces bya'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa zhes/

16b3('bum): ni sgra zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni dri zhes bya'o// 'di ni ro zhes bya'o// 'di ni reg ces bya'o// 'di ni chos zhes bya'o// 'di ni mig gi rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni rna ba'i rnam par shes pa
16b4('bum): zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni sna'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni lce'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni lus kyi rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di
16b5('bum): ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni sku'i 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni lus kyi 'dus
16b6('bum): te reg pa zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni yid kyi 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o//
16b7('bum): 'di ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'dzin
17a1('bum): yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni sa'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni chu'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni me'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni rlung gi//
17a2('bum): khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni nam mkha'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni ma rig pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni 'du byed ces bya'o// 'di ni rnam par
17a3('bum): shes pa zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni ming dang gzugs zhes bya'o// 'di ni skye mched drug ces bya'o// 'di ni reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni sred pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni len
17a4('bum): pa zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni srid pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni skye ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni rga shi zhes bya'o// 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes
17a5('bum): bya'o/ / 'di ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni shes rab kyi pha
17a6('bum): rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni nang stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni phyi stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni phyi nang stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni
17a7('bum): chen po stong pa nyid ces bya'o/ / 'di ni don dam pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni mtha'
17b1('bum): las 'das pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o/ / 'di ni thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di
17b2('bum): ni chos thams cad stong pa nyid ces bya'o/ / 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ces
17b3('bum): bya'o/ / 'di ni ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di dag ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni yang
17b4('bum): dag par spong ba rnams zhes bya'o/ / 'di dag ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni dbang po rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni stobs rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni

17b6('bum): gtan rnams zhes bya'o/ / 'di dag ni tshad med pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni rnam par thar pa brgyad ces
17b7('bum): bya'o/ / 'di dag ni mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa zhes
18a1('bum): bya'o/ / 'di dag ni mngon par shes pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni ting nge 'dzin rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni gzungs kyi sgo rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag/
18a2('bum): ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni mi 'jigs pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni so so yang dag par rig pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di ni byams pa chen
18a3('bum): po zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni snying rje chen po zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams zhes bya'o// 'di ni rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu zhes bya'o// 'di ni lan cig
18a4('bum): phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu zhes bya'o/ / 'di ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu zhes bya'o// 'di ni dgra bcom pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni rang byang chub ces bya'o// 'di ni lam gyi rnam pa
18a5('bum): shes pa nyid ces bya'o/ / 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ces bya'o zhes chos ston to// rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ dper na/ sgyu ma'i mkhan po
18a6('bum): 'am/ sgyu ma byed pa'i mtshan bu mkhas pa zhig gis/ rdzas kyi rnam pa gyi na zhig la brten nas/ gzugs kyi bye brag sna tshogs 'di lta ste/ glang po'i gzugs sam/ rta'i
18a7('bum): gzugs sam/ ba glang gi gzugs sam/ rnga mo dang lug gi gzugs sam/ skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang / bu mo'i gzugs sam/ skyed mos tshal dang
18b1('bum): gzhal med khang dang / dka' thub kyi nags tshal dang / kun dga' ra ba mdangs dga' ba 'am/ rdzing bu mdangs dga' ba 'am/ nags tshal mdangs dga' ba dag sprul cang /
18b2('bum): de dag tu stan dang / 'khor gyi stan dang / gzhi rnam pa sna tshogs btings te/ me tog dang / 'phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pa dang / kha zas dang / spyan gzigs zhim po

37a3('bum): bzhi pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par byams pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par byams pa sgom pa la yang dag par skul ba
37a4('bum): yin/ bdag kyang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par snying rje la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par snying rje sgom pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad
37a5('bum): par dga' ba la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par dga' ba sgom pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par btang snyoms la gnas pa yin//
37a6('bum): gzhan yang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par btang snyoms sgom pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug pa
37a7('bum): yin/ gzhan yang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms
37b1('bum): par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang cung zad med pa'i skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms
37b2('bum): par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang cung zad med pa'i skye mched kyi snyom par 'jug pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa
37b3('bum): la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi snyom par 'jug pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa/
37b4('bum): yin/ gzhan yang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
37b5('bum): la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang brtson
37b6('bum): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin
37b7('bum): gzhan yang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang
38a1('bum): dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang nang stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang nang stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang phyi stong pa nyid sgom pa yin//
38a2('bum): gzhan yang phyi stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang phyi nang stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang phyi nang stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang stong pa nyid
38a3('bum): stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang chen po stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang chen po stong pa nyid la yang dag
38a4('bum): par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang don dam pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang don dam pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'dus byas stong pa nyid sgom pa yin
38a5('bum): gzhan yang 'dus byas stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin
38a6('bum): bdag kyang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid
38a7('bum): sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dor ba med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dor ba med pa stong pa
38b1('bum): nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rang bzhin stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yir/ bdag kyang chos thams cad stong pa
38b2('bum): nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang chos thams cad stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rang gi mtshan nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la
38b3('bum): yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dngos po med pa stong
38b4('bum): pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag
38b5('bum): par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dran pa nye
38b6('bum): bar gzhag pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang yang dag par spong ba rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang yang dag par
38b7('bum): spong ba rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rdza 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang
39a1('bum): dbang po rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dbang po rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang stobs rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stobs rnams la
39a2('bum): yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'phags pa'i lam
39a3('bum): yan lag brgyad pa sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang
39a4('bum): rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin
39a5('bum): bdag kyang rnam par thar pa brgyad la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam par thar pa brgyad la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la slob pa
39a6('bum): yin/ gzhan yang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mngon par shes pa rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mngon par shes
39a7('bum): ba rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang ting nge 'dzin rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang ting nge 'dzin rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang gzungs kyi sgo rnams
39b1('bum): la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang gzungs kyi sgo rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
39b2('bum): bcu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi 'jigs pa bzhi la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mi 'jigs pa bzhi la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang so so yang dag par
39b3('bum): rig pa bzhi la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang byams pa chen po la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang byams pa chen po la
39b4('bum): yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang snying rje chen po la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang snying rje chen po la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la slob
39b5('bum): pa yin/ gzhan yang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mi chen po'i
39b6('bum): mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag
39b7('bum): kyang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i
40a1('bum): shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i shes bskyed
40a2('bum): cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang
40a3('bum): dgra bcom pa nyid la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang rang byang chub kyi shes pa skyed cing de la'ang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rang byang chub la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang bla na med pa yang
40a4('bum): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi lam skyed pa yin/ gzhan yang lam de la 'dems shing rjes su ston pa dang / gzhog cing 'dul ba dang 'god pa yin te/ rab 'byor de ltar byang chub
40a5('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sems dang po bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung ste/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gnas shing sems can rnams kyi
40a6('bum): don byed pa'i tshe/ nam yang las med par gnas pa ma yin no// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te de ltar chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis stong pa lags na/ rab
40a7('bum): bzhin stong pa nyid la ni sems can yang mi dmigs/ chos kyang mi dmigs/ chos ma lags pa'ang mi dmigs na/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen/
40b1('bum): po rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi don du yang dag par 'jug pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ ji skad du smras pa bzhin
40b2('bum): no/ / chos thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong pa ste/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la ni/ sems can mi dmigs so// chos mi dmigs so// chos ma yin pa mi dmigs so// rab 'byor
40b3('bum): gal te chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis stong pa zhig ma yin na ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'ang rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gnas par mi 'gyur te/ bla na med pa yang dag pa
40b4('bum): rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas kyang chos rnams rang bzhin gyis stong par mi ston to/ / rang bzhin gyis stong pa'i chos de dag kyang gang zhe na/ rab 'byor gzugs
40b5('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du shes ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du byed ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //
40b6('bum): rab 'byor mig ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid
40b7('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rab 'byor gzugs ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sgra ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dri ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ro ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // reg ni rang
41a1('bum): bzhin gyis stong ngo / / chos ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig gi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis
41a2('bum): stong ngo / / sna'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi rnam par shes
41a3('bum): pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rab 'byor mig gi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong
41a4('bum): ngo/ / lce'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig gi 'dus
41a5('bum): te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong
41a6('bum): ngo / / lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba
41a7('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rab 'byor sa'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chu'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // me'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rlung gi khams ni
41b1('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / nam mkha'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor ma rig pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du
41b2('bum): byed ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ming dang gzugs ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // skye mched drug ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // reg pa ni rang bzhin
41b3('bum): gyis stong ngo / / tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sred pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // len pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // srid pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // skye ba ni rang bzhin gyis
41b4('bum): stong ngo / / rga shi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bzod pa'i pha
41b5('bum): rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // shes rab kyi pha rol
41b6('bum): tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rab 'byor nang stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi nang stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //
41b7('bum): stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chen po stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // don dam pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin
42a1('bum): gyis stong ngo / / 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid
42a2('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo //
42a3('bum): rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ngo bo nyid stong pa
42a4('bum): nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yang dag par spong
42a5('bum): ba rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dbang po rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // stobs rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // byang

42a7('bum): rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / tshad med pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par thar pa rnams ni

42b6('bum): 'bras bu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo / / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dgra bcom pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis

43a1('bum): 'as na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ phung po lnga ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// skye
43a2('bum): mched bcu gnyis ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to/ / khams bco brgyad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rten cing 'bral par 'byung ba ni rang bzhin gyis
43a3('bum): stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to/ / pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// stong pa nyid thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston te/
43a4('bum): dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi ri rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// yang dag par spong ba bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi ni rang

43a6('bum): yan lag bdun ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to/ / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams ni

43b1('bum): gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rnam par thar pa brgyad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// mthar gyis
43b2('bum): gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to/ / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni rang bzhin

43b4('bum): gzungs kyi sgo thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// mi 'jigs pa bzhini
43b5('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to/ / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// byams pa chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar
43b6('bum): chos ston to/ / snying rje chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// dga' ba chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// btang snyoms chen po ni rang bzhin gyis

113b7('bum): bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhe

114a3('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gis nang stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi nang stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis phyi stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe

114a6('bum): pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi don dam pa stong pa nyid do zhe'am/ bdag gis 'dus byas stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi 'dus byas stong pa nyid de zha
114a7('bum): 'am/ bdag gis 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o//
114b1('bum): zhe 'am/ bdag gi mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid
114b2('bum): do zhe 'am/ bdag gis dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi dor ba med pa stong pa nyid do zhe'am/ bdag gis rang bzhin stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/
114b3('bum): bdag gi rang bzhin stong pa nyid do zhe'am/ bdag gis chos thams cad stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi chos thams cad stong pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis rang gi mtshan
114b4('bum): nyid stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid do zhebs/ bdag gis mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid do zhe

114b7('bum): bdag gis dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis yang dag par spong ba bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe'am
115a1('bum): bdag gi yang dag par spong ba bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag

115b1('bum): / gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rnam par
115b2('bum): thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'o zhe'am/ bdag gis mngon par shes pa rnams la spad par bya'o zhe 'am// bdag gi mngon par shes pa rnams

115b6('bum): par rig pa bzhi'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis byams pa chen po la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi byams pa chen po'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis snying rje chen po la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag

116a1('bum): gis rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'o zhe'am/ bdag gis lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyad
